## Angular

> Angular is a web framework that empowers developers to build fast, reliable applications that users love.

### Official Resources

* [Site](https://angular.dev)
* [Blog](https://blog.angular.dev/)
* [Documentation](https://angular.dev/overview)
* [Getting Started Tutorial](https://angular.dev/tutorials/learn-angular)
* [GitHub Repo](https://github.com/angular/angular) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/angular/angular?style=flat)](https://github.com/angular/angular/stargazers)
* [Past Documentation Site](https://v17.angular.io/docs)

### Builders

* [Webpack](https://webpack.js.org)
* [esbuild](https://esbuild.github.io/)
* [Angular Builders](https://github.com/just-jeb/angular-builders) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/just-jeb/angular-builders?style=flat)](https://github.com/just-jeb/angular-builders/stargazers) - This repo consolidates all the community builders (ES Build, Webpack, Jest, Bazel, and Timestamp) for the Angular build facade.
* [Jest Builder](https://github.com/just-jeb/angular-builders/tree/master/packages/jest) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/just-jeb/angular-builders/tree/master/packages/jest?style=flat)](https://github.com/just-jeb/angular-builders/tree/master/packages/jest/stargazers)
* [Custom Webpack](https://github.com/just-jeb/angular-builders/tree/master/packages/custom-webpack) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/just-jeb/angular-builders/tree/master/packages/custom-webpack?style=flat)](https://github.com/just-jeb/angular-builders/tree/master/packages/custom-webpack/stargazers)
* [Custom esbuild](https://github.com/just-jeb/angular-builders/tree/master/packages/custom-esbuild) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/just-jeb/angular-builders/tree/master/packages/custom-esbuild?style=flat)](https://github.com/just-jeb/angular-builders/tree/master/packages/custom-esbuild/stargazers)
* [Bazel](https://github.com/just-jeb/angular-builders/tree/master/packages/bazel) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/just-jeb/angular-builders/tree/master/packages/bazel?style=flat)](https://github.com/just-jeb/angular-builders/tree/master/packages/bazel/stargazers) - Provides an Angular CLI Builder, which can execute Bazel when triggered by ng build, ng test, etc.
* [Timestamp](https://github.com/just-jeb/angular-builders/tree/master/packages/timestamp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/just-jeb/angular-builders/tree/master/packages/timestamp?style=flat)](https://github.com/just-jeb/angular-builders/tree/master/packages/timestamp/stargazers) - This is explained in this [article](https://medium.com/angular-in-depth/angular-cli-under-the-hood-builders-demystified-v2-e73ee0f2d811).
* [ngx-build-plus](https://github.com/manfredsteyer/ngx-build-plus) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/manfredsteyer/ngx-build-plus?style=flat)](https://github.com/manfredsteyer/ngx-build-plus/stargazers) - Extend the Angular CLI's default build behavior without ejecting, e. g. for Angular Elements.
* [ngx-electronify](https://github.com/bampakoa/ngx-electronify) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bampakoa/ngx-electronify?style=flat)](https://github.com/bampakoa/ngx-electronify/stargazers) - Angular CLI builder that runs your application in the desktop using Electron.
* [dotenv-run](https://github.com/chihab/dotenv-run) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/chihab/dotenv-run?style=flat)](https://github.com/chihab/dotenv-run/stargazers) - Seamlessly load environment variables. Supports cli, esbuild, Rollup, Vite, Webpack, Angular, ESM and Monorepos.
* [ng-packagr](https://github.com/ng-packagr/ng-packagr) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ng-packagr/ng-packagr?style=flat)](https://github.com/ng-packagr/ng-packagr/stargazers) - Compile and package Angular libraries in Angular Package Format (APF).
* [angular-env-builder](https://github.com/igorissen/angular-env-builder) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/igorissen/angular-env-builder?style=flat)](https://github.com/igorissen/angular-env-builder/stargazers) - Builder to generate `src/environments/environment.ts` file based on your environment variables.
* [angular-rspack](https://github.com/nrwl/nx/tree/HEAD/packages/angular-rspack) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nrwl/nx/tree/HEAD/packages/angular-rspack?style=flat)](https://github.com/nrwl/nx/tree/HEAD/packages/angular-rspack/stargazers) - [Rspack](https://github.com/web-infra-dev/rspack) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/web-infra-dev/rspack?style=flat)](https://github.com/web-infra-dev/rspack/stargazers) plugin and tooling for Angular applications.
* [ngx-devkit-builders](https://github.com/Celtian/ngx-devkit-builders) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Celtian/ngx-devkit-builders?style=flat)](https://github.com/Celtian/ngx-devkit-builders/stargazers) - This package contains Architect builders used to build and test Angular applications and libraries.
* [angular-static-assets-hash](https://github.com/sitelint/angular-static-assets-hash) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sitelint/angular-static-assets-hash?style=flat)](https://github.com/sitelint/angular-static-assets-hash/stargazers) - Create a list of Angular static assets and a hash for each file.
* [ngx-schematic-builder](https://github.com/kstepien3/ngx-schematic-builder) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kstepien3/ngx-schematic-builder?style=flat)](https://github.com/kstepien3/ngx-schematic-builder/stargazers) - A tool for building Angular schematic projects. Compiles and packages your custom schematics, preparing them for publishing and use.
* [ng-builder-typescript](https://github.com/da-mkay/ng-builder-typescript) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/da-mkay/ng-builder-typescript?style=flat)](https://github.com/da-mkay/ng-builder-typescript/stargazers) - A builder for the Angular CLI to build Node.js apps using the TypeScript compiler `tsc` (no Webpack or any other bundler used).

### CLI Tools

* [Official website](https://angular.dev/tools/cli)
* [Official GitHub repository](https://github.com/angular/angular-cli) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/angular/angular-cli?style=flat)](https://github.com/angular/angular-cli/stargazers)
* [alterforge](https://github.com/themodulardev/alterforge) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/themodulardev/alterforge?style=flat)](https://github.com/themodulardev/alterforge/stargazers) - A CLI tool that scaffolds and manages modular microservice architectures with optional React or Angular frontends.
* [@MohamedBouattour/angular-clean-architecture](https://github.com/MohamedBouattour/angular-clean-architecture) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/MohamedBouattour/angular-clean-architecture?style=flat)](https://github.com/MohamedBouattour/angular-clean-architecture/stargazers) - A CLI tool that generates Clean Architecture–based, production‑ready Angular features with clear, maintainable layers.
* [angular-cli-diff](https://github.com/cexbrayat/angular-cli-diff) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cexbrayat/angular-cli-diff?style=flat)](https://github.com/cexbrayat/angular-cli-diff/stargazers) - Easily upgrade your Angular CLI applications from one version to another 🚀.
* [angular-cli-ssr-diff](https://github.com/cexbrayat/angular-cli-ssr-diff) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cexbrayat/angular-cli-ssr-diff?style=flat)](https://github.com/cexbrayat/angular-cli-ssr-diff/stargazers) - Easily upgrade your Angular CLI SSR applications from one version to another 🚀.
* [angular-parallel-test-runner](https://github.com/mahdi-hajian/angular-parallel-test-runner) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mahdi-hajian/angular-parallel-test-runner?style=flat)](https://github.com/mahdi-hajian/angular-parallel-test-runner/stargazers) - CLI to run Angular tests in parallel across projects; uses available CPU cores.
* [angular-web-cli](https://github.com/qodalis-solutions/angular-web-cli) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/qodalis-solutions/angular-web-cli?style=flat)](https://github.com/qodalis-solutions/angular-web-cli/stargazers) - A flexible CLI tool designed to streamline workflows, automate tasks, and provide customizable utilities for developers.
* [Better-Fullstack](https://github.com/Marve10s/Better-Fullstack) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Marve10s/Better-Fullstack?style=flat)](https://github.com/Marve10s/Better-Fullstack/stargazers) - Scaffold production-ready fullstack apps in seconds. Pick your stack from 425 options — the CLI wires everything together.
* [dotairc](https://github.com/elecash/dotairc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/elecash/dotairc?style=flat)](https://github.com/elecash/dotairc/stargazers) - This tool helps create consistent instructions for AI assistants working with your codebase.
* [firebase-framework-tools](https://github.com/FirebaseExtended/firebase-framework-tools) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/FirebaseExtended/firebase-framework-tools?style=flat)](https://github.com/FirebaseExtended/firebase-framework-tools/stargazers) - Experimental addon to the [Firebase CLI](https://github.com/firebase/firebase-tools/) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/firebase/firebase-tools/?style=flat)](https://github.com/firebase/firebase-tools//stargazers) to add web framework support.
* [i18n-fixer](https://github.com/zfurkandurum/i18n-fixer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zfurkandurum/i18n-fixer?style=flat)](https://github.com/zfurkandurum/i18n-fixer/stargazers) - Framework-agnostic CLI tool that finds hardcoded strings, missing i18n keys, and unused translations.
* [js-stack](https://github.com/vipinyadav01/js-stack) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vipinyadav01/js-stack?style=flat)](https://github.com/vipinyadav01/js-stack/stargazers) - Modern CLI for scaffolding production-ready JavaScript full-stack projects, with customization and best-practice presets.
* [kqgen](https://github.com/KilloconQ/kqgen) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/KilloconQ/kqgen?style=flat)](https://github.com/KilloconQ/kqgen/stargazers) - A fast and flexible CLI for generating Angular components and services. Includes presets for tables, filters, and for REST/GraphQL services.
* [lin](https://github.com/yuo-app/lin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yuo-app/lin?style=flat)](https://github.com/yuo-app/lin/stargazers) - Lazy I18N is a CLI tool that translates locale JSONs using LLMs.
* [mcp-angular-cli](https://github.com/talzach/mcp-angular-cli) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/talzach/mcp-angular-cli?style=flat)](https://github.com/talzach/mcp-angular-cli/stargazers) - A server offering Angular CLI and workspace automation, enabling LLMs and agents to generate components, add packages, create workspaces, and run custom architect targets.
* [nest-schematics](https://github.com/lcasass3/nest-schematics) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lcasass3/nest-schematics?style=flat)](https://github.com/lcasass3/nest-schematics/stargazers) - An Angular CLI schematic for generating CQRS (Command Query Responsibility Segregation) modules with hexagonal architecture in NestJS.
* [ng-chrome-extension](https://github.com/larscom/ng-chrome-extension) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/larscom/ng-chrome-extension?style=flat)](https://github.com/larscom/ng-chrome-extension/stargazers) - Easily create Angular Chrome Extensions (manifest v3).
* [ng-create-with-config](https://github.com/tranvo-dev/ng-create-with-config) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tranvo-dev/ng-create-with-config?style=flat)](https://github.com/tranvo-dev/ng-create-with-config/stargazers) - A minimal tool to initialize a new Angular project with pre-configured Prettier, ESLint, Husky and Lint-staged.
* [ns-gc](https://github.com/th3n00bc0d3r/ns-gc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/th3n00bc0d3r/ns-gc?style=flat)](https://github.com/th3n00bc0d3r/ns-gc/stargazers) - A lightweight command-line tool to generate standalone NativeScript Angular components and Angular services with clean structure and zero config.
* [ngx-i18n-scan](https://github.com/pratiksonone/ngx-i18n-scan) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pratiksonone/ngx-i18n-scan?style=flat)](https://github.com/pratiksonone/ngx-i18n-scan/stargazers) - A CLI tool that scans Angular code to extract and update i18n translation keys, keeping your translation files clean.
* [ngx-stats](https://github.com/tomer953/ngx-stats) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tomer953/ngx-stats?style=flat)](https://github.com/tomer953/ngx-stats/stargazers) - CLI tool that analyzes Angular projects, quantifying modules, components, directives, pipes, and services to give a clear structural overview for better architectural insight.
* [ngx-ws](https://github.com/art-ws/ngx-ws) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/art-ws/ngx-ws?style=flat)](https://github.com/art-ws/ngx-ws/stargazers) - Easily split a large `angular.json` into modular, project-local files using the power of [JSON References](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@apidevtools/json-schema-ref-parser), with the convenience of [YAML](https://yaml.org/) and [JSON5](https://json5.org/) formats.
* [prepare-angular-json](https://github.com/ackheron/prepare-angular-json) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ackheron/prepare-angular-json?style=flat)](https://github.com/ackheron/prepare-angular-json/stargazers) - A lightweight CLI tool that generates a clean `angular.json` file from a commented `angular.jsonc`.
* [rafacli](https://github.com/rafa00716/rafacli) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rafa00716/rafacli?style=flat)](https://github.com/rafa00716/rafacli/stargazers) - CLI tool that generates authentication and CRUD modules for NestJS and Angular, automating boilerplate to streamline development and ensure consistency.
* [ngx-crafter](https://github.com/ErwanHeschung/ngx-crafter) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ErwanHeschung/ngx-crafter?style=flat)](https://github.com/ErwanHeschung/ngx-crafter/stargazers) - A powerful CLI tool that helps you craft Angular projects with pre-configured folder structures and essential packages.
* [ng new command generator](https://ng.gridatek.com/) - Generate optimized `ng new` commands.
* [svger-cli](https://github.com/faezemohades/svger-cli) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/faezemohades/svger-cli?style=flat)](https://github.com/faezemohades/svger-cli/stargazers) - A lightweight CLI that transforms SVGs into optimized Angular components with zero dependencies.
* [tailwind-init-cli](https://github.com/ImLeoNova/tailwind-init-cli) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ImLeoNova/tailwind-init-cli?style=flat)](https://github.com/ImLeoNova/tailwind-init-cli/stargazers) - A one-command setup tool for Tailwind CSS in Angular, React, or Next.js projects!

### Deployment

* [AWS Amplify](https://docs.amplify.aws/angular/)
* [Vercel](https://vercel.com/solutions/angular)
* [Firebase Hosting](https://firebase.google.com/docs/app-hosting/get-started)
* [Netlify](https://docs.netlify.com/frameworks/angular/) - Angular apps on Netlify gain automatic framework detection and redirects via the [Angular Runtime](https://github.com/netlify/angular-runtime) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/netlify/angular-runtime?style=flat)](https://github.com/netlify/angular-runtime/stargazers) plugin.
* [angular-cli-ghpages](https://github.com/angular-schule/angular-cli-ghpages) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/angular-schule/angular-cli-ghpages?style=flat)](https://github.com/angular-schule/angular-cli-ghpages/stargazers) - SSR does not work, and there can be some caveats, but you can host your Angular project on GitHub Pages.
* [analog-publish-gh-pages](https://github.com/k9n-dev/analog-publish-gh-pages) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/k9n-dev/analog-publish-gh-pages?style=flat)](https://github.com/k9n-dev/analog-publish-gh-pages/stargazers) - A GitHub Action for the Deployment of an `Analog.js` app on GitHub Pages.
* [Genezio](https://github.com/Genez-io/genezio) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Genez-io/genezio?style=flat)](https://github.com/Genez-io/genezio/stargazers) - The easiest way to write and host a serverless application.
* [Cloudflare Pages](https://developers.cloudflare.com/pages/framework-guides/deploy-an-angular-site/#create-a-new-project-using-the-create-cloudflare-cli-c3)
* [Zerops](https://zerops.io/) - It makes deploying and running Analog apps, both [server side rendered](https://github.com/zeropsio/recipe-analog-nodejs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zeropsio/recipe-analog-nodejs?style=flat)](https://github.com/zeropsio/recipe-analog-nodejs/stargazers) and [static](https://github.com/zeropsio/recipe-analog-static) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zeropsio/recipe-analog-static?style=flat)](https://github.com/zeropsio/recipe-analog-static/stargazers), a breeze.
* [SST](https://sst.dev/) - A framework that makes it easy to build and automate modern full-stack applications.
* [ngx-config-orchestrator](https://github.com/xhani-manolis-trungu/ngx-config-orchestrator) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xhani-manolis-trungu/ngx-config-orchestrator?style=flat)](https://github.com/xhani-manolis-trungu/ngx-config-orchestrator/stargazers) - Angular library for runtime configuration via external JSON, enabling “Build Once, Deploy Anywhere.”
* [deploy-with-git](https://github.com/RunOnFlux/deploy-with-git/tree/master/deploy-angular) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RunOnFlux/deploy-with-git/tree/master/deploy-angular?style=flat)](https://github.com/RunOnFlux/deploy-with-git/tree/master/deploy-angular/stargazers) - Lets you deploy an Angular app directly to the [Flux Network](https://runonflux.com/) from a Git repository.
* [@railwayapp-templates/angular-starter](https://github.com/railwayapp-templates/angular-starter) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/railwayapp-templates/angular-starter?style=flat)](https://github.com/railwayapp-templates/angular-starter/stargazers) - One-click default Angular TS starter, utilizing Caddy to serve!
* [angular-deploy-bunny](https://github.com/lostium/angular-deploy-bunny) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lostium/angular-deploy-bunny?style=flat)](https://github.com/lostium/angular-deploy-bunny/stargazers) - Angular Architect builder (`ng deploy`) that syncs your build to a Bunny.net CDN Storage Zone using SHA256 incremental diffing, then purges the corresponding Pull Zone.
* [ngx-ssh-deploy](https://bitbucket.org/dkhang97/ngx-ssh-deploy/src/master/) - Deploy Angular projects using SSH.

### Desktop Applications

* [electron](https://github.com/electron/electron) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/electron/electron?style=flat)](https://github.com/electron/electron/stargazers) - Build cross-platform desktop apps with JavaScript, HTML, and CSS.
* [angular-electron](https://github.com/maximegris/angular-electron) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/maximegris/angular-electron?style=flat)](https://github.com/maximegris/angular-electron/stargazers) - Ultra-fast bootstrapping with Angular and Electron.
* [neutralinojs](https://github.com/neutralinojs/neutralinojs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/neutralinojs/neutralinojs?style=flat)](https://github.com/neutralinojs/neutralinojs/stargazers) - A lightweight, portable framework for building cross‑platform desktop apps with JavaScript, HTML, and CSS, running on Linux, macOS, Windows, Web, and Chrome.
* [nw.js](https://github.com/nwjs/nw.js) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nwjs/nw.js?style=flat)](https://github.com/nwjs/nw.js/stargazers) - Chromium + Node.js runtime for native apps using HTML, JavaScript, and direct Node integration.
* [nw-angular-example](https://github.com/nwutils/nw-angular-example) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nwutils/nw-angular-example?style=flat)](https://github.com/nwutils/nw-angular-example/stargazers) - An example of integrating Angular with NW.js.
* [tauri](https://v2.tauri.app/) - Create small, fast, secure, cross-platform applications.
* [angular-tauri](https://github.com/maximegris/angular-tauri) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/maximegris/angular-tauri?style=flat)](https://github.com/maximegris/angular-tauri/stargazers) - Ultra-fast bootstrapping with Angular and Tauri.
* [create-tauri-app](https://github.com/tauri-apps/create-tauri-app) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tauri-apps/create-tauri-app?style=flat)](https://github.com/tauri-apps/create-tauri-app/stargazers) - Rapidly scaffold out a new Tauri app project.
* [wails](https://github.com/wailsapp/wails) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/wailsapp/wails?style=flat)](https://github.com/wailsapp/wails/stargazers) - Build desktop applications using Go & web technologies, including [Angular](https://wails.io/docs/guides/angular/).
* [MōBrowser](https://teamdev.com/mobrowser) - A framework for building desktop apps using TypeScript, HTML, and CSS, with source code protection built in.

### Updating Angular

* [Official website](https://angular.dev/update-guide) - Interactive guide to help you migrate from one version of Angular to another.  
* [Official update reference](https://angular.dev/cli/update) - Use the CLI to update your project or try new Angular features by adding the `--next` flag.
* [Official migrations reference](https://angular.dev/reference/migrations) - Angular schematics help update projects by enabling conversion to standalone components, new control flow syntax, and more.
* [ng-morph](https://github.com/taiga-family/ng-morph) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/taiga-family/ng-morph?style=flat)](https://github.com/taiga-family/ng-morph/stargazers) - Code mutations in your project or schematics were never easier than now.
* [ngx-libs](https://github.com/eneajaho/ngx-libs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/eneajaho/ngx-libs?style=flat)](https://github.com/eneajaho/ngx-libs/stargazers) - Angular Libraries Support lists community libs support for each Angular version.
* [@fast-facts/ng-update](https://github.com/fast-facts/ng-update) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fast-facts/ng-update?style=flat)](https://github.com/fast-facts/ng-update/stargazers) - A GitHub Action that keeps your Angular CLI-based projects up-to-date via automated PRs based on `ng update`.
* [npx-app-updater](https://github.com/DSI-HUG/ngx-app-updater) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DSI-HUG/ngx-app-updater?style=flat)](https://github.com/DSI-HUG/ngx-app-updater/stargazers) - Alerts users to available updates when a new version is deployed.
* [ngx-update-app](https://github.com/Celtian/ngx-update-app) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Celtian/ngx-update-app?style=flat)](https://github.com/Celtian/ngx-update-app/stargazers) - Angular directive for updating app via service workers.
* [Angular Caniuse](https://www.angular.courses/caniuse/features) - Track Angular features from preview to stable stages.
* [Depfixer](https://depfixer.com/sample-report/angular) - Smart dependency analysis for JS/TS projects; detects compatibility conflicts and provides step‑by‑step fixes.
* [migration-planificator](https://github.com/silvestv/migration-planificator-documentation) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/silvestv/migration-planificator-documentation?style=flat)](https://github.com/silvestv/migration-planificator-documentation/stargazers) - Plan Angular migrations with precision AST analysis, calculate workload estimates, and generate interactive HTML dashboards.
* [NgReady](https://www.ngready.dev/) - Stop Wasting Days on Angular Upgrades.

## Architecture and Advanced Topics

### Feature Flags

* [OpenFeature Angular SDK](https://openfeature.dev/docs/reference/technologies/client/web/angular) - A vendor-agnostic, community-driven API specification for feature flagging.
* [@devcycle/openfeature-angular-provider](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@devcycle/openfeature-angular-provider) - [DevCycle](https://docs.devcycle.com/sdk/client-side-sdks/angular/) supports the OpenFeature Angular SDK.
* [@openfeature/go-feature-flag-web-provider](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@openfeature/go-feature-flag-web-provider) - [GO Feature Flag](https://gofeatureflag.org/) provider allows you to [connect](https://gofeatureflag.org/docs/sdk/client_providers/openfeature_angular) to your GO Feature Flag instance with the `@openfeature/web-sdk`.
* [Flagsmith](https://www.flagsmith.com/) - Ship Faster and Control Releases with Feature Flag Management.
* [@statsig/angular-bindings](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@statsig/angular-bindings) - The [Statsig](https://www.statsig.com/) Angular bindings package provides a `StatsigService` that can be injected into your components. See the [Statsig docs](https://docs.statsig.com/client/javascript-sdk/Angular/) for more details.
* [@configcat/js-sdk](https://github.com/configcat/js-sdk) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/configcat/js-sdk?style=flat)](https://github.com/configcat/js-sdk/stargazers) - ConfigCat SDK for JavaScript provides easy integration for your application to [ConfigCat](https://configcat.com/).
* [@configcat-labs/feature-flags-in-angular-sample-app](https://github.com/configcat-labs/feature-flags-in-angular-sample-app) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/configcat-labs/feature-flags-in-angular-sample-app?style=flat)](https://github.com/configcat-labs/feature-flags-in-angular-sample-app/stargazers) - Example app that uses ConfigCat.
* [featurit-sdk-angular](https://github.com/featurit/featurit-sdk-angular) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/featurit/featurit-sdk-angular?style=flat)](https://github.com/featurit/featurit-sdk-angular/stargazers) - Angular wrapper of the JavaScript client for the [FeaturIT](https://featurit.com/) Feature Flag management platform.
* [ngx-feature-proxy](https://github.com/zenkiet/ngx-feature-proxy) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zenkiet/ngx-feature-proxy?style=flat)](https://github.com/zenkiet/ngx-feature-proxy/stargazers) - Angular feature flag library with Unleash; reactive and type-safe flag management with minimal setup.
* [ngx-feature-flags](https://github.com/pavan-98/ngx-feature-flags) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pavan-98/ngx-feature-flags?style=flat)](https://github.com/pavan-98/ngx-feature-flags/stargazers) - An Angular‑first, enterprise‑ready feature‑flag layer that standardizes how flags are resolved, guarded, and rendered across Angular apps.
* [ngx-feature-flags-toggly](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@ops-ai/ngx-feature-flags-toggly) - Angular SDK for [Toggly](https://toggly.io/) feature flags.
* [ngx-circuit](https://github.com/pjlamb12/ngx-circuit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pjlamb12/ngx-circuit?style=flat)](https://github.com/pjlamb12/ngx-circuit/stargazers) - Streamlines feature‑toggle management with flexible options like boolean flags and percentage rollouts.
* [ngx-feature-toggle](https://github.com/willmendesneto/ngx-feature-toggle) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/willmendesneto/ngx-feature-toggle?style=flat)](https://github.com/willmendesneto/ngx-feature-toggle/stargazers) - Simplify managing feature toggles with this Angular directive.
* [@rollgate/sdk-angular](https://github.com/rollgate/sdks/tree/main/packages/sdk-angular) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rollgate/sdks/tree/main/packages/sdk-angular?style=flat)](https://github.com/rollgate/sdks/tree/main/packages/sdk-angular/stargazers) - Angular SDK for [Rollgate](https://rollgate.io), a feature‑flag platform with scheduled releases and gradual rollouts.

### GraphQL

* [apollo-angular](https://github.com/kamilkisiela/apollo-angular) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kamilkisiela/apollo-angular?style=flat)](https://github.com/kamilkisiela/apollo-angular/stargazers) - A fully-featured, production ready caching GraphQL client for Angular and every GraphQL server.
* [apollo-dynamic-angular](https://github.com/giuliano-marinelli/apollo-dynamic-angular) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/giuliano-marinelli/apollo-dynamic-angular?style=flat)](https://github.com/giuliano-marinelli/apollo-dynamic-angular/stargazers) - Variant of Apollo Angular that allows dynamic selection sets for queries, mutations and subscriptions via a decorated schema.
* [apollo-orbit](https://github.com/wassim-k/apollo-orbit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/wassim-k/apollo-orbit?style=flat)](https://github.com/wassim-k/apollo-orbit/stargazers) - A fully-featured GraphQL client for Angular with modular state management.
* [buoy](https://github.com/buoy-graphql/buoy) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/buoy-graphql/buoy?style=flat)](https://github.com/buoy-graphql/buoy/stargazers) - A GraphQL client for Angular built on top of Apollo.
* [graphql-code-generator](https://github.com/dotansimha/graphql-code-generator) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dotansimha/graphql-code-generator?style=flat)](https://github.com/dotansimha/graphql-code-generator/stargazers) - Code generator for GraphQL schemas and operations, with flexible plugin support.
* [ngx-graphql-client](https://github.com/Alevettih/ngx-graphql-client) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Alevettih/ngx-graphql-client?style=flat)](https://github.com/Alevettih/ngx-graphql-client/stargazers) - A typed GraphQL client for Angular applications with full TypeScript support.
* [takeshape](https://www.takeshape.io/) - It's easy to build a GraphQL API using TakeShape. Follow this [guide](https://app.takeshape.io/docs/get-started/client/angular) to integrate with Angular.

### HTTP

* [ng-http-caching](https://github.com/nigrosimone/ng-http-caching) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nigrosimone/ng-http-caching?style=flat)](https://github.com/nigrosimone/ng-http-caching/stargazers) - Cache for HTTP requests in Angular application.
* [@ngify/http](https://github.com/ngify/ngify/tree/main/packages/http) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ngify/ngify/tree/main/packages/http?style=flat)](https://github.com/ngify/ngify/tree/main/packages/http/stargazers) - Reactive Angular HTTP client with typed responses, streamlined errors, and request/response interception.
* [ng-http-loader](https://github.com/mpalourdio/ng-http-loader) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mpalourdio/ng-http-loader?style=flat)](https://github.com/mpalourdio/ng-http-loader/stargazers) - Smart Angular HTTP interceptor - Intercepts automagically HTTP requests and shows a spinkit spinner / loader / progress bar.
* [angular-odata](https://github.com/diegomvh/angular-odata) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/diegomvh/angular-odata?style=flat)](https://github.com/diegomvh/angular-odata/stargazers) - A fluent API for querying, creating, updating and deleting OData resources in Angular.
* [ng-memento](https://github.com/terzurumluoglu/ng-memento) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/terzurumluoglu/ng-memento?style=flat)](https://github.com/terzurumluoglu/ng-memento/stargazers) - Makes your application faster by preventing the same HTTP requests from being called again in your Angular project.
* [ngx-suspense-of](https://github.com/Celtian/ngx-suspense-of) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Celtian/ngx-suspense-of?style=flat)](https://github.com/Celtian/ngx-suspense-of/stargazers) - Angular directive that adds suspense to your app.
* [ngx-pwa](https://github.com/Service-Soft/ngx-pwa) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Service-Soft/ngx-pwa?style=flat)](https://github.com/Service-Soft/ngx-pwa/stargazers) - Provides additional functionality around Angular PWA's. Most notably being able to cache and sync POST/PATCH/DELETE Requests.
* [ngx-repository](https://github.com/paddls/ngx-repository) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/paddls/ngx-repository?style=flat)](https://github.com/paddls/ngx-repository/stargazers) - Easily create a strongly typed data client (HTTP REST or Firestore) in your Angular project.
* [ng-rest-client](https://github.com/gizm0bill/gzm/tree/master/libs/ng-rest-client) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gizm0bill/gzm/tree/master/libs/ng-rest-client?style=flat)](https://github.com/gizm0bill/gzm/tree/master/libs/ng-rest-client/stargazers) - This library simplifies HTTP requests by letting developers define RESTful API clients with method decorators.
* [ngx-sse-client](https://github.com/marcospds/ngx-sse-client) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/marcospds/ngx-sse-client?style=flat)](https://github.com/marcospds/ngx-sse-client/stargazers) - A simple **SSE** (Server Sent Events) client for Angular applications to replace the use of `EventSource`.
* [@connectrpc/connect-web](https://github.com/connectrpc/connect-es/tree/main/packages/connect-web) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/connectrpc/connect-es/tree/main/packages/connect-web?style=flat)](https://github.com/connectrpc/connect-es/tree/main/packages/connect-web/stargazers) - [Connect](https://connectrpc.com/) provides cross-platform API libraries. [@connectrpc/connect](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@connectrpc/connect) offers type-safe Protobuf APIs in TypeScript, and [@connectrpc/connect-web](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@connectrpc/connect-web) adds browser support. See the [Angular example](https://github.com/connectrpc/examples-es/tree/main/angular) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/connectrpc/examples-es/tree/main/angular?style=flat)](https://github.com/connectrpc/examples-es/tree/main/angular/stargazers).
* [ng-httpclient-easy-network-stub](https://github.com/NGneers/ng-httpclient-easy-network-stub) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/NGneers/ng-httpclient-easy-network-stub?style=flat)](https://github.com/NGneers/ng-httpclient-easy-network-stub/stargazers) - An easy class to mock a lot of network requests from the Angular HttpClient.
* [simply-direct](https://github.com/fvilli/simply-direct) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fvilli/simply-direct?style=flat)](https://github.com/fvilli/simply-direct/stargazers) - A fullstack communication library that bridges Angular and NestJS through real-time, bidirectional communication powered by WebSockets.
* [ng-error-handling](https://github.com/ressurectit/ng-error-handling) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ressurectit/ng-error-handling?style=flat)](https://github.com/ressurectit/ng-error-handling/stargazers) - An Angular module designed for managing HTTP API error responses.
* [active-connect](https://github.com/HiptJo/active-connect) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/HiptJo/active-connect?style=flat)](https://github.com/HiptJo/active-connect/stargazers) - A connection framework for Node.js, Angular, and WebSockets that simplifies real-time client–server communication with decorators and utilities.
* [ngx-signal-pagination](https://github.com/JPtenBerge/ngx-signal-pagination) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/JPtenBerge/ngx-signal-pagination?style=flat)](https://github.com/JPtenBerge/ngx-signal-pagination/stargazers) - Pagination for Angular, powered by signals.
* [ngx-http](https://github.com/OGS-GmbH/ngx-http) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/OGS-GmbH/ngx-http?style=flat)](https://github.com/OGS-GmbH/ngx-http/stargazers) - A lightweight Angular library that enhances HTTP functionalities by providing types, static values, and utility functions.
* [ng-speed-test](https://github.com/jrquick17/ng-speed-test) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jrquick17/ng-speed-test?style=flat)](https://github.com/jrquick17/ng-speed-test/stargazers) - A lightweight Angular library for checking internet speed.
* [ngx-interceptors](https://github.com/SebaRenner/ngx-interceptors) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SebaRenner/ngx-interceptors?style=flat)](https://github.com/SebaRenner/ngx-interceptors/stargazers) - Library with common HTTP interceptors for Angular applications.
* [ngx-hal](https://github.com/infinum/ngx-hal) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/infinum/ngx-hal?style=flat)](https://github.com/infinum/ngx-hal/stargazers) - A datastore library with support for handling [HAL-formatted](http://stateless.co/hal_specification.html) HTTP requests.
* [trpc-angular](https://github.com/heddendorp/trpc-angular) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/heddendorp/trpc-angular?style=flat)](https://github.com/heddendorp/trpc-angular/stargazers) - This repository offers two tRPC-based Angular packages: `@heddendorp/trpc-link-angular` for HttpClient, and `@heddendorp/tanstack-angular-query` for reactive data fetching.
* [my-http-resource](https://github.com/consoleLogMyAss/my-http-resource/tree/main/projects/my-http-resource) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/consoleLogMyAss/my-http-resource/tree/main/projects/my-http-resource?style=flat)](https://github.com/consoleLogMyAss/my-http-resource/tree/main/projects/my-http-resource/stargazers) - A reactive Angular HttpClient wrapper that streamlines requests by managing state, URL parameters, and configuration.
* [luminara](https://github.com/miller-28/luminara) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/miller-28/luminara?style=flat)](https://github.com/miller-28/luminara/stargazers) - A modern, universal HTTP client built on native fetch, designed for reliable, scalable, and clear architecture.
* [ngx-cachr](https://github.com/nulzo/ngx-cachr) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nulzo/ngx-cachr?style=flat)](https://github.com/nulzo/ngx-cachr/stargazers) - A slim, signal-based caching library for Angular.
* [ngx-data-polling](https://github.com/antonio-spinelli/ngx-data-polling) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/antonio-spinelli/ngx-data-polling?style=flat)](https://github.com/antonio-spinelli/ngx-data-polling/stargazers) - Angular library with utilities to handle data polling in a declarative and type-safe way.
* [ngx-soap](https://github.com/seyfer/ngx-soap) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/seyfer/ngx-soap?style=flat)](https://github.com/seyfer/ngx-soap/stargazers) - A lightweight SOAP client built on [node‑soap](https://github.com/vpulim/node-soap) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vpulim/node-soap?style=flat)](https://github.com/vpulim/node-soap/stargazers), fully compatible with Angular’s signals, standalone components, and modern features.
* [ngx-http-fetch-tracking](https://github.com/pegasusheavy/ngx-http-fetch-tracking) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pegasusheavy/ngx-http-fetch-tracking?style=flat)](https://github.com/pegasusheavy/ngx-http-fetch-tracking/stargazers) - Angular library providing upload progress tracking for the Fetch API backend.
* [fetchquack](https://github.com/adrian-bueno/fetchquack) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/adrian-bueno/fetchquack?style=flat)](https://github.com/adrian-bueno/fetchquack/stargazers) - Angular‑ready HTTP client with an RxJS Observable wrapper and injection‑context support, offering lightweight Fetch‑based streaming, SSE, and upload/download progress handling.
* [ziflux](https://github.com/neogenz/ziflux) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/neogenz/ziflux?style=flat)](https://github.com/neogenz/ziflux/stargazers) - A zero‑dependency, signal‑native caching layer for Angular 21+ with stale‑while‑revalidate for resource()—instant navigations, background refreshes, no spinners.
* [ng-signal-query](https://github.com/Ali7040/ng-signal-query) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Ali7040/ng-signal-query?style=flat)](https://github.com/Ali7040/ng-signal-query/stargazers) - A type‑safe Angular querying library built on signals that streamlines server state, infinite queries, mutations, and caching with high performance.
* [api-caller](https://forge.deejayy.hu/angular-packages/api-caller) - Simple API caller library for Angular.
* [ngx-lite-cache](https://github.com/Suleeyman/ngx-lite-cache) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Suleeyman/ngx-lite-cache?style=flat)](https://github.com/Suleeyman/ngx-lite-cache/stargazers) - An Angular library that caches HTTP responses via HttpClient interceptors to cut redundant requests and boost performance.
* [ng-qubee](https://github.com/AndreaAlhena/ng-qubee) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AndreaAlhena/ng-qubee?style=flat)](https://github.com/AndreaAlhena/ng-qubee/stargazers) - Angular query builder with reactive URIs (RxJS + Signals), typed pagination, 495+ tests, and multi‑driver support.
* [ngx-trpc-client](https://github.com/BeGj/ngx-trpc-client) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/BeGj/ngx-trpc-client?style=flat)](https://github.com/BeGj/ngx-trpc-client/stargazers) - Reworked fork of Analog's [TRPC package](https://github.com/analogjs/analog/tree/beta/packages/trpc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/analogjs/analog/tree/beta/packages/trpc?style=flat)](https://github.com/analogjs/analog/tree/beta/packages/trpc/stargazers).
* [zx-angular-lazy-resource](https://github.com/zxnc/zx-angular-lazy-resource) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zxnc/zx-angular-lazy-resource?style=flat)](https://github.com/zxnc/zx-angular-lazy-resource/stargazers) - Lazy helpers for Angular's signal-based `resource()` — defer loading until first access, and await the first settled value as a promise.

### Micro-Frontends

* [angular-microfrontend-demo](https://github.com/gioboa/angular-microfrontend-demo) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gioboa/angular-microfrontend-demo?style=flat)](https://github.com/gioboa/angular-microfrontend-demo/stargazers) - Module Federation Vite + Angular is now possible.
* [backbase-micro-frontends](https://github.com/Backbase/backbase-micro-frontends) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Backbase/backbase-micro-frontends?style=flat)](https://github.com/Backbase/backbase-micro-frontends/stargazers) - Proof of concept showcasing how legacy apps (widgets) can work together with newer apps (journeys) via Module Federation.
* [micro-frontends-mindmaps](https://github.com/santoshshinde2012/micro-frontends-mindmaps) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/santoshshinde2012/micro-frontends-mindmaps?style=flat)](https://github.com/santoshshinde2012/micro-frontends-mindmaps/stargazers) - A mindmap summarizing micro-frontends concepts.
* [ngx-mfe](https://github.com/dkhrunov/ngx-mfe) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dkhrunov/ngx-mfe?style=flat)](https://github.com/dkhrunov/ngx-mfe/stargazers) - Angular library for working with micro-frontends in Webpack 5 and plugin ModuleFederation.

### Module Federation

* [@module-federation/core](https://github.com/module-federation/core) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/module-federation/core?style=flat)](https://github.com/module-federation/core/stargazers) - Module Federation is a concept that allows developers to share code and resources across multiple JavaScript applications.
* [ng-dynamic-mf](https://github.com/LoaderB0T/ng-dynamic-mf) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/LoaderB0T/ng-dynamic-mf?style=flat)](https://github.com/LoaderB0T/ng-dynamic-mf/stargazers) - Truly dynamic modules at runtime with Module Federation.
* [module-federation-plugin](https://github.com/angular-architects/module-federation-plugin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/angular-architects/module-federation-plugin?style=flat)](https://github.com/angular-architects/module-federation-plugin/stargazers) - Plugin integrating Module Federation with Angular CLI for loading micro frontends or plugins.
* [webpack-module-federation-with-angular](https://github.com/edumserrano/webpack-module-federation-with-angular) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/edumserrano/webpack-module-federation-with-angular?style=flat)](https://github.com/edumserrano/webpack-module-federation-with-angular/stargazers) - Guide to learn about Webpack Module Federation with several Angular code demos.
* [Vite-module-federation-angular-test](https://github.com/Seifenn/vite-module-federation-angular-test) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Seifenn/vite-module-federation-angular-test?style=flat)](https://github.com/Seifenn/vite-module-federation-angular-test/stargazers) - Tests [Module Federation Vite](https://github.com/module-federation/vite) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/module-federation/vite?style=flat)](https://github.com/module-federation/vite/stargazers) with Angular and AnalogJS (via [@brandonroberts/angular-vite](https://github.com/brandonroberts/angular-vite) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/brandonroberts/angular-vite?style=flat)](https://github.com/brandonroberts/angular-vite/stargazers)); explores SSR with an AnalogJS host (plugin SSR support may vary).
* [mfe-crossframework](https://github.com/igorhms/mfe-crossframework) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/igorhms/mfe-crossframework?style=flat)](https://github.com/igorhms/mfe-crossframework/stargazers) - Module Federation project with Angular Host, Cross-framework remotes and without Nx.
* [npm-mfe-live-reload](https://www.npmjs.com/package/npm-mfe-live-reload) - This tool auto-reloads the shell in development mode when remote microfrontends change.

### Monorepos

* [Moon](https://moonrepo.dev/docs/guides/examples/angular) - A Rust-based build and monorepo management tool for the web.
* [Nx](https://github.com/nrwl/nx) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nrwl/nx?style=flat)](https://github.com/nrwl/nx/stargazers) - A build system with integrated tools and advanced CI features for maintaining and scaling monorepos locally and in CI.
* [Turbo](https://github.com/vercel/turbo) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vercel/turbo?style=flat)](https://github.com/vercel/turbo/stargazers) - Turbopack (Rust bundler) and Turborepo (build system/monorepo tools) for JavaScript and TypeScript.

### Server-Side Rendering

* [Official website](https://angular.dev/guide/ssr#enable-server-side-rendering) - Documentation for the new SSR package built into the framework.
* [angular-prerender](https://github.com/chrisguttandin/angular-prerender) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/chrisguttandin/angular-prerender?style=flat)](https://github.com/chrisguttandin/angular-prerender/stargazers) - A command line tool to prerender Angular Apps.
* [analogjs](https://analogjs.org/) - Fullstack Angular meta-framework supports both server-side rendering (SSR) and static site generation (SSG) of Angular applications.
* [bot-ssr](https://github.com/patrikx3/bot-ssr) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/patrikx3/bot-ssr?style=flat)](https://github.com/patrikx3/bot-ssr/stargazers) - SSR for bots, instant CSR for users — fast loads and clean prerendered HTML for major crawlers, powered by [isbot](https://github.com/omrilotan/isbot) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/omrilotan/isbot?style=flat)](https://github.com/omrilotan/isbot/stargazers).
* [ngx-sitemaps](https://github.com/json-derulo/ngx-sitemaps) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/json-derulo/ngx-sitemaps?style=flat)](https://github.com/json-derulo/ngx-sitemaps/stargazers) - Generate sitemaps from Angular prerendered routes.
* [ngx-bun](https://github.com/pegasusheavy/ngx-bun) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pegasusheavy/ngx-bun?style=flat)](https://github.com/pegasusheavy/ngx-bun/stargazers) - High-performance SSR/SSG adapter for Angular 19+ using Bun's built-in server.

## Development Utilities

### Accessibility

* [Official Angular ARIA](https://angular.dev/guide/aria/overview) - A collection of headless, accessible directives that implement common WAI-ARIA patterns.
* [digital.gov](https://digital.gov/guides/accessibility-for-teams/) - Accessibility for teams guide from USA government.
* [WAI](https://www.w3.org/WAI/) - The W3C Web Accessibility Initiative (WAI) develops standards and support materials to help you understand and implement accessibility.
* [webaim](https://webaim.org/) - Web accessibility in mind.
* [WAVE](https://wave.webaim.org/) - Web Accessibility Evaluation Tools.
* [axe Accessibility Linter](https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=deque-systems.vscode-axe-linter) - Accessibility linting for HTML, Angular, React, Markdown, Vue, and React Native.
* [Angular Material CDK - a11y](https://material.angular.io/cdk/a11y/overview) - The a11y package provides a number of tools to improve accessibility.
* [PrimeNG](https://primeng.org/guides/accessibility) - Accessibility guide from PrimeNG.
* [astral-accessibility](https://github.com/verto-health/astral-accessibility) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/verto-health/astral-accessibility?style=flat)](https://github.com/verto-health/astral-accessibility/stargazers) - An open-source accessibility widget written in Angular.
* [angular-vlibras](https://github.com/angular-a11y/angular-vlibras) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/angular-a11y/angular-vlibras?style=flat)](https://github.com/angular-a11y/angular-vlibras/stargazers) - An Angular library that integrates VLibras to automatically translate content into Brazilian Sign Language (Libras).
* [a11y-libraries](https://github.com/LDV2k3/a11y-libraries) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/LDV2k3/a11y-libraries?style=flat)](https://github.com/LDV2k3/a11y-libraries/stargazers) - A range of accessibility solutions for Angular.
* [a11yguard](https://github.com/shamaz332/a11yguard) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/shamaz332/a11yguard?style=flat)](https://github.com/shamaz332/a11yguard/stargazers) - Delivers a zero‑dependency accessibility toolkit with cross‑framework primitives, idiomatic adapters, and a runtime audit mapped to EAA / EN 301 549.
* [ulam](https://github.com/mikeyil/ulam) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mikeyil/ulam?style=flat)](https://github.com/mikeyil/ulam/stargazers) - Accessibility utilities for the modern web. Vanilla-first, with optional React, Remix, Vue, and Angular adapters.
* [aria-reach](https://github.com/manichandra/aria-reach) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/manichandra/aria-reach?style=flat)](https://github.com/manichandra/aria-reach/stargazers) - ARIA accessibility anti-pattern analyzer for shared component libraries.

* [panda](https://github.com/chakra-ui/panda) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/chakra-ui/panda?style=flat)](https://github.com/chakra-ui/panda/stargazers) - Easily use Panda, CSS-in-JS Framework, with Angular with its dedicated [integration](https://panda-css.com/docs/docs/installation/angular).
* [prime-ng-theme-fe](https://github.com/mkccl/prime-ng-theme-fe) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mkccl/prime-ng-theme-fe?style=flat)](https://github.com/mkccl/prime-ng-theme-fe/stargazers) - A visual theme designer for PrimeNG.
* [Super JSS](https://github.com/rsantoyo-dev/super-jss-workspace) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rsantoyo-dev/super-jss-workspace?style=flat)](https://github.com/rsantoyo-dev/super-jss-workspace/stargazers) - Super JavaScript Stylesheets is a tiny Angular runtime library that generates atomic CSS with breakpoints and theming.
* [Theme-Kit](https://github.com/M1tsumi/Theme-Kit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/M1tsumi/Theme-Kit?style=flat)](https://github.com/M1tsumi/Theme-Kit/stargazers) - A unified design‑token SDK that centralizes your colors, typography, and spacing for seamless use across React, Vue, Angular, or any JavaScript project.
* [tokiforge](https://github.com/TokiForge/tokiforge) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/TokiForge/tokiforge?style=flat)](https://github.com/TokiForge/tokiforge/stargazers) - Framework-agnostic design token engine for React, Vue, Angular, Svelte & vanilla JS.

Provides reactive session handling with signals, clean DI provider setup with observables, and modern guards.

* [casl-angular](https://github.com/stalniy/casl/tree/master/packages/casl-angular) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stalniy/casl/tree/master/packages/casl-angular?style=flat)](https://github.com/stalniy/casl/tree/master/packages/casl-angular/stargazers) - Module which integrates isomorphic permissions management library [CASL](https://github.com/stalniy/casl) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stalniy/casl?style=flat)](https://github.com/stalniy/casl/stargazers) with Angular.

### Security Best Practices

* [Official Angular Security](https://angular.dev/best-practices/security) - Best Practices.
* [Aikido](https://www.aikido.dev/) - Secure your code, cloud, and runtime in one central system. Find and fix vulnerabilities automatically.
* [GitHub Code Scanning](https://docs.github.com/en/code-security/concepts/code-scanning) - Learn core concepts for GitHub's code scanning features.
* [GitHub Skills](https://skills.github.com/) - Guided interactive tutorials for Code Security and analysis are available.
* [HackTricks](https://book.hacktricks.xyz/network-services-pentesting/pentesting-web/angular) - Angular Security  Checklist.
* [SafeDep](https://safedep.io/) - It continuously scans open source code for vulnerabilities and malware, helping security engineering teams proactively mitigate inherited OSS risks.
* [Snyk](https://snyk.io/) - A developer security platform that integrates directly into development tools, workflows, and automation pipelines.
* [Socket](https://socket.dev/) - A developer-first security platform that protects your code from both vulnerable and malicious dependencies.
* [supply-chain-inspector](https://github.com/DenysVuika/supply-chain-inspector) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DenysVuika/supply-chain-inspector?style=flat)](https://github.com/DenysVuika/supply-chain-inspector/stargazers) - A standalone, zero-dependency Node.js script for supply chain security analysis of npm dependencies.
* [Vulert](https://vulert.com) - Secures software by detecting vulnerabilities in open-source dependencies—without accessing your code. It supports JS, PHP, Java, Python, and more.

### NgRx

* [ngrx-rtk-query](https://github.com/SaulMoro/ngrx-rtk-query) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SaulMoro/ngrx-rtk-query?style=flat)](https://github.com/SaulMoro/ngrx-rtk-query/stargazers) - Make RTK Query with Hooks works in Angular Applications.
* [angular-ngrx-nx-realworld-example-app](https://github.com/stefanoslig/angular-ngrx-nx-realworld-example-app) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stefanoslig/angular-ngrx-nx-realworld-example-app?style=flat)](https://github.com/stefanoslig/angular-ngrx-nx-realworld-example-app/stargazers) - Real world application built with Angular 21, NgRx 21, and Nx 22.
* [ngx-view-state](https://github.com/yurakhomitsky/ngx-view-state) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yurakhomitsky/ngx-view-state?style=flat)](https://github.com/yurakhomitsky/ngx-view-state/stargazers) - Library for handling Loading/Success/Error in NgRx.
* [store-service](https://github.com/ngxp/store-service) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ngxp/store-service?style=flat)](https://github.com/ngxp/store-service/stargazers) - Adds an abstraction layer / facade between Angular components and the NgRx store.
* [ngx-signal-store-query](https://github.com/k3nsei/ngx-signal-store-query) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/k3nsei/ngx-signal-store-query?style=flat)](https://github.com/k3nsei/ngx-signal-store-query/stargazers) - Signal Store feature that bridges with [Angular Query](https://tanstack.com/query/latest/docs/framework/angular/overview).
* [SmartNgRX](https://github.com/DaveMBush/SmartNgRX) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DaveMBush/SmartNgRX?style=flat)](https://github.com/DaveMBush/SmartNgRX/stargazers) - A library that simplifies CRUD operations by abstracting NgRx, while still leveraging and supporting existing NgRx code.
* [ngrx-hateoas](https://github.com/angular-architects/ngrx-hateoas) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/angular-architects/ngrx-hateoas?style=flat)](https://github.com/angular-architects/ngrx-hateoas/stargazers) - A library to bring hypermedia json into the NgRx Signal Store following the HATEOAS approach.
* [ngrx-http-tracking](https://github.com/acandylevey/ngrx-http-tracking) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/acandylevey/ngrx-http-tracking?style=flat)](https://github.com/acandylevey/ngrx-http-tracking/stargazers) - This NgRx library integrates with existing stores to reduce boilerplate and simplify handling HTTP request states like loading, success, and error.
* [ngrx-set](https://github.com/parloti/ngrx-set) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/parloti/ngrx-set?style=flat)](https://github.com/parloti/ngrx-set/stargazers) - This simplifies the creation of actions for asynchronous requests that can succeed, fail, or be aborted.
* [easy-ngrx-distinct-selector](https://github.com/NGneers/easy-ngrx-distinct-selector) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/NGneers/easy-ngrx-distinct-selector?style=flat)](https://github.com/NGneers/easy-ngrx-distinct-selector/stargazers) - Provides functions to easily create `@ngrx/store` selectors with equal functions for arguments and result values.
* [ngrx-store-wrapper](https://github.com/himanshuarora111/ngrx-store-wrapper) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/himanshuarora111/ngrx-store-wrapper?style=flat)](https://github.com/himanshuarora111/ngrx-store-wrapper/stargazers) - Angular library for NgRx state management with built-in session and local storage, no manual actions or reducers needed.
* [ngx-rehydrate](https://github.com/solidexpert-ltd/ngx-rehydrate) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/solidexpert-ltd/ngx-rehydrate?style=flat)](https://github.com/solidexpert-ltd/ngx-rehydrate/stargazers) - NgRx state rehydration library for Angular SSR applications.

### NGXS

* [Official website](https://www.ngxs.io/)
* [Official GitHub repository](https://github.com/ngxs/store) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ngxs/store?style=flat)](https://github.com/ngxs/store/stargazers) - NGXS aims to simplify state management with minimal boilerplate and maintenance.
* [action-lifecycle-hooks](https://github.com/ngxs-labs/action-lifecycle-hooks) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ngxs-labs/action-lifecycle-hooks?style=flat)](https://github.com/ngxs-labs/action-lifecycle-hooks/stargazers) - Makes it simple to trigger code on action outcomes—such as success or error—without manual action wiring.
* [actions-executing](https://github.com/ngxs-labs/actions-executing) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ngxs-labs/actions-executing?style=flat)](https://github.com/ngxs-labs/actions-executing/stargazers) - This plugin allows you to easily know if an action is being executed and control UI elements or control flow of your code to execute.
* [emitter](https://github.com/ngxs-labs/emitter) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ngxs-labs/emitter?style=flat)](https://github.com/ngxs-labs/emitter/stargazers) - New pattern that provides the opportunity to feel free from actions.
* [firestore-plugin](https://github.com/ngxs-labs/firestore-plugin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ngxs-labs/firestore-plugin?style=flat)](https://github.com/ngxs-labs/firestore-plugin/stargazers) - Firestore plugin for NGXS.
* [ngxs-postmessage-plugin](https://github.com/nelsongraa8/ngxs-postmessage-plugin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nelsongraa8/ngxs-postmessage-plugin?style=flat)](https://github.com/nelsongraa8/ngxs-postmessage-plugin/stargazers) - NGXS plugin for state synchronization across windows or microfrontends using `postMessage`.
* [ngxs-synchronizers](https://github.com/lVlyke/ngxs-synchronizers) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lVlyke/ngxs-synchronizers?style=flat)](https://github.com/lVlyke/ngxs-synchronizers/stargazers) - Simplifies synchronizing your NGXS-based application state with external data sources.

### Other State Libraries

* [ng-simple-state](https://github.com/nigrosimone/ng-simple-state) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nigrosimone/ng-simple-state?style=flat)](https://github.com/nigrosimone/ng-simple-state/stargazers) - Simple state management in Angular with only services and RxJS.

* [TanStack Query](https://github.com/TanStack/query) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/TanStack/query?style=flat)](https://github.com/TanStack/query/stargazers) - Powerful asynchronous state management, server-state utilities and data fetching for the web.

* [xstate](https://github.com/statelyai/xstate) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/statelyai/xstate?style=flat)](https://github.com/statelyai/xstate/stargazers) - Actor-based state management & orchestration for complex app logic.
* [signalstory](https://github.com/zuriscript/signalstory) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zuriscript/signalstory?style=flat)](https://github.com/zuriscript/signalstory/stargazers) - A state management library built on Angular signals, supporting simple repositories, decoupled commands, side effects, and inter-store communication via event-driven architecture.
* [ngx-sherlock](https://github.com/politie/ngx-sherlock) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/politie/ngx-sherlock?style=flat)](https://github.com/politie/ngx-sherlock/stargazers) - An Angular tooling library to be used with the [@politie/sherlock](https://github.com/politie/sherlock) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/politie/sherlock?style=flat)](https://github.com/politie/sherlock/stargazers) distributed reactive state management library.
* [tansu](https://github.com/AmadeusITGroup/tansu) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AmadeusITGroup/tansu?style=flat)](https://github.com/AmadeusITGroup/tansu/stargazers) - A lightweight, push-based state management library. It works well with [the Angular ecosystem](https://amadeusitgroup.github.io/tansu/#md:tansu-works-well-with-the-angular-ecosystem).
* [@tethys/store](https://github.com/worktile/store) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/worktile/store?style=flat)](https://github.com/worktile/store/stargazers) - A mini, yet powerful state management library for Angular.
* [ngx-crud](https://github.com/henryruhs/ngx-crud) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/henryruhs/ngx-crud?style=flat)](https://github.com/henryruhs/ngx-crud/stargazers) - CRUD services in Angular with effortless aborting, caching and observing.

* [ngx-query](https://github.com/CoreSyncHub/ngx-query) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/CoreSyncHub/ngx-query?style=flat)](https://github.com/CoreSyncHub/ngx-query/stargazers) - A lightweight, observable-based query library that helps you manage server state, caching, and synchronization between your backend and UI.
* [@tanstack/angular-db](https://github.com/TanStack/db/tree/main/packages/angular-db) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/TanStack/db/tree/main/packages/angular-db?style=flat)](https://github.com/TanStack/db/tree/main/packages/angular-db/stargazers) - Angular hooks for TanStack DB, a reactive client store that lets you build fast, sync‑driven apps with a backend‑agnostic real‑time data layer.

* [ngx-mxstore](https://github.com/MaxxtonGroup/ngx-mxstore) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/MaxxtonGroup/ngx-mxstore?style=flat)](https://github.com/MaxxtonGroup/ngx-mxstore/stargazers) - Simplifies state management by moving logic into pure, testable methods and connecting components to the store via decorators.
* [ngx-stashr](https://github.com/nulzo/ngx-stashr) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nulzo/ngx-stashr?style=flat)](https://github.com/nulzo/ngx-stashr/stargazers) - A lightweight, signal-driven state management library for Angular 21, inspired by React’s [Zustand](https://github.com/pmndrs/zustand) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pmndrs/zustand?style=flat)](https://github.com/pmndrs/zustand/stargazers).
* [ngx-event-bus-lib](https://github.com/orelnatan/ngx-event-bus-lib) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/orelnatan/ngx-event-bus-lib?style=flat)](https://github.com/orelnatan/ngx-event-bus-lib/stargazers) - Broadcast strongly-typed events anywhere in your app and react to them declaratively — without services, DI, providers, RxJS, signals, or tight coupling.
* [rs-x](https://github.com/robert-sanders-software-ontwikkeling/rs-x) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/robert-sanders-software-ontwikkeling/rs-x?style=flat)](https://github.com/robert-sanders-software-ontwikkeling/rs-x/stargazers) - A reactive engine that unifies sync and async data into one transparent model, giving Angular fine‑grained automatic change detection without manual async handling.
* [stateloom](https://github.com/sujeet-pro/stateloom) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sujeet-pro/stateloom?style=flat)](https://github.com/sujeet-pro/stateloom/stargazers) - A universal state‑management SDK featuring a signal‑driven reactive core, along with paradigm adapters (Store, Atom, Proxy) and framework adapters for React, Angular, and more.
* [ngx-state-crafter](https://github.com/irvrodflo/ngx-state-crafter) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/irvrodflo/ngx-state-crafter?style=flat)](https://github.com/irvrodflo/ngx-state-crafter/stargazers) - A lightweight, signal‑driven state library for Angular with a clean, boilerplate‑free API.
* [coaction](https://github.com/coactionjs/coaction) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/coactionjs/coaction?style=flat)](https://github.com/coactionjs/coaction/stargazers) - An efficient and flexible state management library for building high-performance, multithreading web applications.
* [flurryx](https://github.com/fmflurry/flurryx) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fmflurry/flurryx?style=flat)](https://github.com/fmflurry/flurryx/stargazers) - A signal-first reactive state toolkit for Angular that bridges RxJS streams into structured, cache-aware stores.
* [ngStato](https://github.com/becher/ngStato) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/becher/ngStato?style=flat)](https://github.com/becher/ngStato/stargazers) - State management for Angular that uses async/await instead of RxJS.
* [ng-eagleeye.js](https://github.com/webKrafters/ng-eagleeye.js) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/webKrafters/ng-eagleeye.js?style=flat)](https://github.com/webKrafters/ng-eagleeye.js/stargazers) - A framework-agnostic, native JavaScript immutable state manager with change-streams, deployable anywhere.
* [ngx-deep-signals](https://github.com/simplesoftsoul/ngx-deep-signals) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/simplesoftsoul/ngx-deep-signals?style=flat)](https://github.com/simplesoftsoul/ngx-deep-signals/stargazers) - Deeply reactive, zero‑ceremony nested state for Angular—turn any object into a signal graph without calls, setters, or boilerplate.

## Testing

### E2E

* [Cypress](https://www.cypress.io/) - End to End and Component Testing for Angular.
* [cypress-harness](https://github.com/jscutlery/devkit/tree/main/packages/cypress-harness) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jscutlery/devkit/tree/main/packages/cypress-harness?style=flat)](https://github.com/jscutlery/devkit/tree/main/packages/cypress-harness/stargazers) - This library provides Cypress support to Component Test Harnesses.
* [cypress-angular-commands](https://github.com/MohamedSci/cypress-angular-commands) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/MohamedSci/cypress-angular-commands?style=flat)](https://github.com/MohamedSci/cypress-angular-commands/stargazers) - A production-ready collection of reusable Cypress custom commands for modern Angular enterprise and ERP applications.
* [lib-e2e-cypress-for-dummys](https://github.com/GonzaloCarmenado/lib-e2e-cypress-for-dummys) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/GonzaloCarmenado/lib-e2e-cypress-for-dummys?style=flat)](https://github.com/GonzaloCarmenado/lib-e2e-cypress-for-dummys/stargazers) - An Angular library that automatically records the Cypress commands needed to test your application while you browse and use the interface.
* [testcafe](https://testcafe.io/) - A user-friendly end-to-end testing solution.
* [webdriverio](https://github.com/webdriverio/webdriverio) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/webdriverio/webdriverio?style=flat)](https://github.com/webdriverio/webdriverio/stargazers) - Next-gen browser and mobile automation test framework for Node.js.
* [Puppeteer Angular Schematic](https://pptr.dev/guides/ng-schematics) - Adds [Puppeteer-based](https://github.com/puppeteer/puppeteer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/puppeteer/puppeteer?style=flat)](https://github.com/puppeteer/puppeteer/stargazers) e2e tests to your Angular project.
* [ngx-playwright](https://github.com/bgotink/ngx-playwright) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bgotink/ngx-playwright?style=flat)](https://github.com/bgotink/ngx-playwright/stargazers) - Tools to run Playwright e2e tests in an Angular workspace.
* [playwright-ng-schematics](https://github.com/jfgreffier/playwright-ng-schematics) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jfgreffier/playwright-ng-schematics?style=flat)](https://github.com/jfgreffier/playwright-ng-schematics/stargazers) - Adds Playwright Test to your Angular project.
* [playwright-coverage](https://github.com/bgotink/playwright-coverage) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bgotink/playwright-coverage?style=flat)](https://github.com/bgotink/playwright-coverage/stargazers) - Report coverage on Playwright tests using v8 coverage, without requiring any instrumentation.
* [Cypress to Playwright](https://www.cy2pw.com/) - A curated collection of resources that can help you to migrate your test suite from Cypress to Playwright.
* [Playwright Chrome Recorder](https://chromewebstore.google.com/detail/playwright-chrome-recorde/bfnbgoehgplaehdceponclakmhlgjlpd) - Export Chromium recorder tab data to Playwright tests. This gives you a nice starting point that you can refine to modern Playwright.
* [playwright-mcp](https://github.com/microsoft/playwright-mcp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/microsoft/playwright-mcp?style=flat)](https://github.com/microsoft/playwright-mcp/stargazers) - A Model Context Protocol (MCP) server that provides browser automation capabilities using Playwright.
* [twd](https://github.com/BRIKEV/twd) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/BRIKEV/twd?style=flat)](https://github.com/BRIKEV/twd/stargazers) - In‑browser test runner with instant feedback, Testing Library support, Vite discovery, and built‑in API mocking—framework‑agnostic and easy to use in Angular.

### Component

* [Angular Testing Library](https://testing-library.com/docs/angular-testing-library/intro/) - Extends DOM Testing Library by introducing APIs tailored for testing Angular components.

* [Meticulous AI](https://www.meticulous.ai/) - Cover the 1000s of edge cases of your application - without writing or maintaining a single test.
* [Jasmine](https://jasmine.github.io/) - Simple JavaScript testing.
* [docker-ng-cli-karma](https://github.com/trion-development/docker-ng-cli-karma) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/trion-development/docker-ng-cli-karma?style=flat)](https://github.com/trion-development/docker-ng-cli-karma/stargazers) - Angular Docker image capable of running Karma with Chrome.

* [jest-preset-angular](https://github.com/thymikee/jest-preset-angular) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/thymikee/jest-preset-angular?style=flat)](https://github.com/thymikee/jest-preset-angular/stargazers) - Jest configuration preset for Angular projects.
* [jest-preview](https://github.com/nvh95/jest-preview) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvh95/jest-preview?style=flat)](https://github.com/nvh95/jest-preview/stargazers) - Debug your Jest tests. Effortlessly.
* [jest-marbles](https://github.com/just-jeb/jest-marbles) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/just-jeb/jest-marbles?style=flat)](https://github.com/just-jeb/jest-marbles/stargazers) - Helpers library for marbles testing with Jest.
* [jest-codemods](https://github.com/skovhus/jest-codemods) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/skovhus/jest-codemods?style=flat)](https://github.com/skovhus/jest-codemods/stargazers) - Codemods for migrating to Jest.
* [ts-jest](https://github.com/kulshekhar/ts-jest) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kulshekhar/ts-jest?style=flat)](https://github.com/kulshekhar/ts-jest/stargazers) - A Jest transformer with source map support that lets you use Jest to test projects written in TypeScript.
* [Vitest](https://vitest.dev/) - A Vite-native testing framework.
* [Early AI](https://www.startearly.ai/) - Save time, enhance code coverage, and ensure quality with Early's automatically generated, verified, and validated unit tests. Works with Jest and Vitest.
* [swc-angular](https://github.com/jscutlery/devkit/tree/main/packages/swc-angular) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jscutlery/devkit/tree/main/packages/swc-angular?style=flat)](https://github.com/jscutlery/devkit/tree/main/packages/swc-angular/stargazers) - This is a set of Angular presets that enable you to use SWC (Speedy Web Compiler) with Jest or Vitest.
* [swc-angular-plugin](https://github.com/jscutlery/devkit/tree/main/packages/swc-angular-plugin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jscutlery/devkit/tree/main/packages/swc-angular-plugin?style=flat)](https://github.com/jscutlery/devkit/tree/main/packages/swc-angular-plugin/stargazers) - SWC (Speedy Web Compiler) is a lightning-fast JavaScript/TypeScript compiler, but it doesn't support Angular so you need this plugin.
* [wdio-harness](https://github.com/badisi/wdio-harness) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/badisi/wdio-harness?style=flat)](https://github.com/badisi/wdio-harness/stargazers) - WebdriverIO support for Angular component test harnesses.
* [testronaut](https://github.com/testronaut/testronaut) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/testronaut/testronaut?style=flat)](https://github.com/testronaut/testronaut/stargazers) - By removing mocks and guesswork, [Testronaut](https://testronaut.github.io/testronaut/) enables developers to visually inspect output and write precise tests with Playwright’s robust API.

### Helpers

* [Official Angular Material CDK Testing](https://material.angular.dev/cdk/testing/overview) - `@angular/cdk/testing` provides infrastructure to help with testing Angular components.
* [ng-mocks](https://github.com/help-me-mom/ng-mocks) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/help-me-mom/ng-mocks?style=flat)](https://github.com/help-me-mom/ng-mocks/stargazers) - Angular testing library for mocking components, directives, pipes, services and facilitating TestBed setup.
* [ng-mocks-sandbox](https://github.com/help-me-mom/ng-mocks-sandbox) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/help-me-mom/ng-mocks-sandbox?style=flat)](https://github.com/help-me-mom/ng-mocks-sandbox/stargazers) - A repo with guides and examples for unit tests in Angular applications using ng-mocks.
* [spectacular](https://github.com/ngworker/ngworker/tree/main/packages/spectacular) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ngworker/ngworker/tree/main/packages/spectacular?style=flat)](https://github.com/ngworker/ngworker/tree/main/packages/spectacular/stargazers) - Offers test harnesses for Angular applications and libraries.
* [ngx-page-object-model](https://github.com/FrancescoBorzi/ngx-page-object-model) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/FrancescoBorzi/ngx-page-object-model?style=flat)](https://github.com/FrancescoBorzi/ngx-page-object-model/stargazers) - This library simplifies Angular UI component testing using the Page Object Model (POM), separating test logic from DOM manipulation for better abstraction.
* [ngtx](https://github.com/Centigrade/ngtx) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Centigrade/ngtx?style=flat)](https://github.com/Centigrade/ngtx/stargazers) - A**ng**ular **T**esting E**x**tensions is a small set of functions that make your life easier when testing Angular components.
* [ngx-testing-tools](https://github.com/remscodes/ngx-testing-tools) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/remscodes/ngx-testing-tools?style=flat)](https://github.com/remscodes/ngx-testing-tools/stargazers) - Provides high-level utilities and reduces boilerplate for testing Angular applications.

You will find this library useful for unit, integration, and e2e testing.

* [elements-template](https://github.com/giacomo/elements-template) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/giacomo/elements-template?style=flat)](https://github.com/giacomo/elements-template/stargazers) - A modern, opinionated starter kit for building custom Web Components powered by Angular 21, Tailwind CSS v4, and Vitest.
* [realworld-angular](https://github.com/realworld-angular/realworld-angular) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/realworld-angular/realworld-angular?style=flat)](https://github.com/realworld-angular/realworld-angular/stargazers) - RealWorld Angular example apps showcasing Angular libraries in action.
* [spartan-admin-dashboard](https://github.com/Oussemasahbeni/spartan-admin-dashboard) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Oussemasahbeni/spartan-admin-dashboard?style=flat)](https://github.com/Oussemasahbeni/spartan-admin-dashboard/stargazers) - A production-ready, Angular admin dashboard template built with Spartan UI components and Tailwind CSS.
