* [Admin Mart](https://adminmart.com/templates/angular-dashboard/)
* [CozyDevKit](https://cozydevkit.com/) - Interactive tools, architecture patterns, cheat sheets, and DevOps services for Angular 21.

### Captcha

* [altcha](https://github.com/altcha-org/altcha) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/altcha-org/altcha?style=flat)](https://github.com/altcha-org/altcha/stargazers) - GDPR, WCAG 2.2 AA, and EAA compliant, self-hosted CAPTCHA alternative with PoW mechanism and advanced anti-spam filter.
* [go-captcha-angular](https://github.com/wenlng/go-captcha-angular) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/wenlng/go-captcha-angular?style=flat)](https://github.com/wenlng/go-captcha-angular/stargazers) - A simple, easy-to-use, interactive, and secure behavioral verification code that implements verification modes such as text/graphic clicking, sliding/dragging, and rotation.
* [ng-cloudflare-turnstile](https://github.com/pangz-lab/ng-cloudflare-turnstile) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pangz-lab/ng-cloudflare-turnstile?style=flat)](https://github.com/pangz-lab/ng-cloudflare-turnstile/stargazers) - An intuitive, lightweight and easy to integrate [Cloudflare turnstile](https://developers.cloudflare.com/turnstile/) component for Angular.
* [ng-hcaptcha](https://github.com/leNicDev/ng-hcaptcha) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/leNicDev/ng-hcaptcha?style=flat)](https://github.com/leNicDev/ng-hcaptcha/stargazers) - Provides an easy to use component for [hCaptcha](https://hcaptcha.com/).
* [ng-recaptcha-2](https://github.com/LakhveerChahal/ng-recaptcha-2) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/LakhveerChahal/ng-recaptcha-2?style=flat)](https://github.com/LakhveerChahal/ng-recaptcha-2/stargazers) - Angular 18 fork of [ng-recaptcha](https://github.com/DethAriel/ng-recaptcha) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DethAriel/ng-recaptcha?style=flat)](https://github.com/DethAriel/ng-recaptcha/stargazers). Alternatively, you create your own service that implements Google's reCAPTCHA with the help of this [article](https://ben-5.azurewebsites.net/2024/9/5/google-recaptcha-v3-with-angular/#google_vignette).
* [ngx-captcha-kit](https://github.com/edward124689/ngx-captcha-kit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/edward124689/ngx-captcha-kit?style=flat)](https://github.com/edward124689/ngx-captcha-kit/stargazers) - This kit simplifies CAPTCHA implementation with a single component and service, ensuring compatibility with Angular 20+ features like Signals and zoneless change detection.
* [ngx-dice-captcha](https://github.com/Easy-Cloud-in/ngx-dice-captcha) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Easy-Cloud-in/ngx-dice-captcha?style=flat)](https://github.com/Easy-Cloud-in/ngx-dice-captcha/stargazers) - A dynamic 3D CAPTCHA library featuring dice-based interaction and lifelike physics powered by Three.js and Cannon-es.
* [ngx-easy-captcha](https://github.com/angx-libs/ngx-easy-captcha) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/angx-libs/ngx-easy-captcha?style=flat)](https://github.com/angx-libs/ngx-easy-captcha/stargazers) - Easy captcha implementation for both Google Recaptcha and Cloudflare Turnstile.
* [ngx-numeric-captcha](https://github.com/ShreyashThorat-17/ngx-numeric-captcha) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ShreyashThorat-17/ngx-numeric-captcha?style=flat)](https://github.com/ShreyashThorat-17/ngx-numeric-captcha/stargazers) - A modern, lightweight Angular CAPTCHA library featuring multiple verification challenges.
* [ngx-turnstile](https://github.com/verto-health/ngx-turnstile) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/verto-health/ngx-turnstile?style=flat)](https://github.com/verto-health/ngx-turnstile/stargazers) - Cloudflare Turnstile for Angular.
* [trustcaptcha-angular](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@trustcomponent/trustcaptcha-angular) - This library helps you [integrate](https://docs.trustcaptcha.com/en/frontend/integration?frontend=angular) [Trustcaptcha](https://www.trustcaptcha.com/en) into your Angular frontend applications.
* [yandex-smart-captcha](https://github.com/ngx-rock/yandex-smart-captcha) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ngx-rock/yandex-smart-captcha?style=flat)](https://github.com/ngx-rock/yandex-smart-captcha/stargazers) - An Angular library for integrating [Yandex SmartCaptcha](https://yandex.cloud/en/services/smartcaptcha) with support for standard/invisible captchas, reactive forms, and modern signals/effects.

### Data Grids

* [ag-grid](https://www.ag-grid.com/) - The best JavaScript Data Table for building Enterprise Applications. Supports React, Angular, Vue and Plain JavaScript.
* [ignite-ui-angular's grid](https://www.infragistics.com/products/ignite-ui-angular/angular/components/grid/grid) - The data grid, tree grid, hierarchical grid in `Ignite UI` provide excel-style filtering, live-data, sorting, draggable row and other toolbar.
* [sheetjs](https://docs.sheetjs.com/docs/demos/frontend/angular) - A JavaScript library for reading and writing data from spreadsheets.
* [active-table](https://github.com/OvidijusParsiunas/active-table) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/OvidijusParsiunas/active-table?style=flat)](https://github.com/OvidijusParsiunas/active-table/stargazers) - Framework agnostic table component for editable data experience.
* [jsgrids](https://github.com/statico/jsgrids) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/statico/jsgrids?style=flat)](https://github.com/statico/jsgrids/stargazers) - A comparison tool to compare JavaScript data grid and spreadsheet libraries.  Find even more libraries from this repo.
* [handsontable](https://handsontable.com/docs/javascript-data-grid/angular-installation/) - A popular JavaScript data grid component that brings the well-known look and feel of spreadsheets to your application.
* [slickgrid-universal](https://github.com/ghiscoding/slickgrid-universal) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ghiscoding/slickgrid-universal?style=flat)](https://github.com/ghiscoding/slickgrid-universal/stargazers) - A monorepo which includes all editors, filters, extensions, and services related to framework agnostic [SlickGrid](https://github.com/6pac/SlickGrid) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/6pac/SlickGrid?style=flat)](https://github.com/6pac/SlickGrid/stargazers) usage.
* [revogrid](https://github.com/revolist/revogrid) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/revolist/revogrid?style=flat)](https://github.com/revolist/revogrid/stargazers) - Powerful virtual data grid smartsheet with advanced customization. Best features from Excel plus incredible performance.

The library can be used in [Angular](https://www.zinggrid.com/docs/integrations/js-frameworks-&-libs/angular) and many more frameworks.
* [ngx-panemu-table](https://github.com/panemu/ngx-panemu-table) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/panemu/ngx-panemu-table?style=flat)](https://github.com/panemu/ngx-panemu-table/stargazers) - An Angular table component. It is designed to be easy to use. Most work will be in TypeScript file, while the HTML file only needs to have a very simple `panemu-table` tag.

* [angular-inport](https://github.com/ajaysinghj8/angular-inport) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ajaysinghj8/angular-inport?style=flat)](https://github.com/ajaysinghj8/angular-inport/stargazers) - Angular In-Viewport Detector.

### Drag and Drop

* [Official Angular Docs](https://angular.dev/guide/drag-drop)
* [ngx-drag-drop](https://github.com/reppners/ngx-drag-drop) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/reppners/ngx-drag-drop?style=flat)](https://github.com/reppners/ngx-drag-drop/stargazers) - Angular directives using the native HTML Drag And Drop API.

* [ngx-swapy](https://github.com/omnedia/ngx-swapy) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/omnedia/ngx-swapy?style=flat)](https://github.com/omnedia/ngx-swapy/stargazers) - A simple component library to get a drag and drop DOM through the help of [Swapy](https://github.com/TahaSh/swapy) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/TahaSh/swapy?style=flat)](https://github.com/TahaSh/swapy/stargazers).
* [ngx-draggable-dom](https://github.com/bmartinson/ngx-draggable-dom) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bmartinson/ngx-draggable-dom?style=flat)](https://github.com/bmartinson/ngx-draggable-dom/stargazers) - Angular attribute directive that causes any element to become a draggable element.

* [ngx-puzzle](https://github.com/zhongmiao-org/ngx-puzzle) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zhongmiao-org/ngx-puzzle?style=flat)](https://github.com/zhongmiao-org/ngx-puzzle/stargazers) - Drag-and-drop dashboard builder for Angular applications.

* [ngx-markdown-pages](https://github.com/jamesmandrews/ngx-markdown-pages) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jamesmandrews/ngx-markdown-pages?style=flat)](https://github.com/jamesmandrews/ngx-markdown-pages/stargazers) - An Angular library for rendering markdown files as routable pages.
* [ngx-md-editable](https://codeberg.org/tomaszatoo/ngx-md-editable) - A lightweight Angular component that edits Markdown and renders expressive HTML content.
* [ngx-remark](https://github.com/ericleib/ngx-remark) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ericleib/ngx-remark?style=flat)](https://github.com/ericleib/ngx-remark/stargazers) - Render markdown with custom Angular templates.
* [ngx-streamdown](https://github.com/dina-kar/ngx-streamdown) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dina-kar/ngx-streamdown?style=flat)](https://github.com/dina-kar/ngx-streamdown/stargazers) - Angular port of [Streamdown](https://streamdown.ai/), a streaming Markdown renderer optimized for AI‑driven applications.
* [mark-down](https://github.com/mzebley/mark-down) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mzebley/mark-down?style=flat)](https://github.com/mzebley/mark-down/stargazers) - A framework‑agnostic snippet engine with an Angular adapter that indexes Markdown at build time and renders HTML at runtime with optional sanitization.
* [m-render](https://github.com/Foblex/m-render) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Foblex/m-render?style=flat)](https://github.com/Foblex/m-render/stargazers) - A library for rendering Markdown with extended support for Angular components and code snippets.

* [ngx-tippy-wrapper](https://github.com/farengeyt451/ngx-tippy-wrapper) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/farengeyt451/ngx-tippy-wrapper?style=flat)](https://github.com/farengeyt451/ngx-tippy-wrapper/stargazers) - Angular wrapper for [Tippy.js](https://github.com/atomiks/tippyjs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/atomiks/tippyjs?style=flat)](https://github.com/atomiks/tippyjs/stargazers).

* [ngx-smart-tooltip](https://github.com/techasif/ngx-smart-tooltip) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/techasif/ngx-smart-tooltip?style=flat)](https://github.com/techasif/ngx-smart-tooltip/stargazers) - A lightweight, customizable tooltip library for Angular 18 that uses signals, the Web Animations API, and OnPush change detection.

* [ngx-gauge](https://github.com/ashish-chopra/ngx-gauge) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ashish-chopra/ngx-gauge?style=flat)](https://github.com/ashish-chopra/ngx-gauge/stargazers) - A highly customizable Gauge component for Angular apps and dashboards.
* [ngx-glassy-effect](https://github.com/anassmdi/ngx-glassy-effect) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/anassmdi/ngx-glassy-effect?style=flat)](https://github.com/anassmdi/ngx-glassy-effect/stargazers) - An Angular directive that applies a glassy effect to your HTML elements.
* [ngx-globe](https://github.com/omnedia/ngx-globe) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/omnedia/ngx-globe?style=flat)](https://github.com/omnedia/ngx-globe/stargazers) - A simple component library to create a container with an animated globe.
* [ngx-gooey](https://github.com/wadie/ngx-gooey) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/wadie/ngx-gooey?style=flat)](https://github.com/wadie/ngx-gooey/stargazers) - The gooey effect for Angular, used for shape blobbing / metaballs.
* [ngx-lamp](https://github.com/omnedia/ngx-lamp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/omnedia/ngx-lamp?style=flat)](https://github.com/omnedia/ngx-lamp/stargazers) - A simple component library to create a lamp.

## Underlying Technologies

### RxJS

* [Official website](https://rxjs.dev/) - Reactive Extensions Library for JavaScript.
* [eslint-plugin-rxjs-x](https://github.com/JasonWeinzierl/eslint-plugin-rxjs-x) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/JasonWeinzierl/eslint-plugin-rxjs-x?style=flat)](https://github.com/JasonWeinzierl/eslint-plugin-rxjs-x/stargazers) - Fork of [eslint-plugin-rxjs](https://github.com/cartant/eslint-plugin-rxjs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cartant/eslint-plugin-rxjs?style=flat)](https://github.com/cartant/eslint-plugin-rxjs/stargazers) adding ESLint flat config support with breaking changes and improvements.
* [learn-rxjs](https://github.com/btroncone/learn-rxjs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/btroncone/learn-rxjs?style=flat)](https://github.com/btroncone/learn-rxjs/stargazers) - Clear examples, explanations, and resources for RxJS.
* [ng-event-bus](https://github.com/cristiammercado/ng-event-bus) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cristiammercado/ng-event-bus?style=flat)](https://github.com/cristiammercado/ng-event-bus/stargazers) - RxJS-based message bus service for Angular.
* [ngx-device-permission](https://github.com/PhilipSh/ngx-device-permission) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/PhilipSh/ngx-device-permission?style=flat)](https://github.com/PhilipSh/ngx-device-permission/stargazers) - Angular library for handling device permissions (camera, microphone, geolocation, etc.) in a reactive way using RxJS.
* [ngx-operators](https://github.com/nilsmehlhorn/ngx-operators) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nilsmehlhorn/ngx-operators?style=flat)](https://github.com/nilsmehlhorn/ngx-operators/stargazers) - RxJS operators for Angular.
* [ngx-safe-subscribe](https://github.com/Badisi/ngx-safe-subscribe) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Badisi/ngx-safe-subscribe?style=flat)](https://github.com/Badisi/ngx-safe-subscribe/stargazers) - Easy way to automatically unsubscribe from RxJS observables in Angular components.
* [operators](https://github.com/jscutlery/devkit/tree/main/packages/operators) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jscutlery/devkit/tree/main/packages/operators?style=flat)](https://github.com/jscutlery/devkit/tree/main/packages/operators/stargazers) - This package regroups a couple of RxJS operators meant to simplify some common patterns.
* [reactive-event-source](https://github.com/andreasnicolaou/reactive-event-source) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/andreasnicolaou/reactive-event-source?style=flat)](https://github.com/andreasnicolaou/reactive-event-source/stargazers) - Lightweight RxJS-based EventSource wrapper with auto-reconnect, leak prevention, and reactive state management.
* [redux-observable](https://github.com/redux-observable/redux-observable) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/redux-observable/redux-observable?style=flat)](https://github.com/redux-observable/redux-observable/stargazers) - RxJS middleware for action side effects in Redux using "Epics".
* [rx-computed](https://github.com/jscutlery/devkit/tree/main/packages/rx-computed) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jscutlery/devkit/tree/main/packages/rx-computed?style=flat)](https://github.com/jscutlery/devkit/tree/main/packages/rx-computed/stargazers) - The async RxJS-based version of signals' `computed()`.
* [@mrOranger/RxJs](https://github.com/mrOranger/RxJs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mrOranger/RxJs?style=flat)](https://github.com/mrOranger/RxJs/stargazers) - Theory with examples about the Reactive Programming paradigm, using the library RxJS.
* [rxjs-broker](https://github.com/chrisguttandin/rxjs-broker) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/chrisguttandin/rxjs-broker?style=flat)](https://github.com/chrisguttandin/rxjs-broker/stargazers) - An RxJS message broker for WebRTC DataChannels and WebSockets.
* [rxjs-challenge](https://github.com/AngularWave/rxjs-challenge) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AngularWave/rxjs-challenge?style=flat)](https://github.com/AngularWave/rxjs-challenge/stargazers) - A set of little RxJS puzzles to practice your Observable skills.
* [rxjs-collection](https://github.com/henryruhs/rxjs-collection) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/henryruhs/rxjs-collection?style=flat)](https://github.com/henryruhs/rxjs-collection/stargazers) - RxJS enhanced Array, Map, WeakMap, Set, and WeakSet.
* [rxjs-common](https://github.com/paddls/rxjs-common) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/paddls/rxjs-common?style=flat)](https://github.com/paddls/rxjs-common/stargazers) - A collection of useful RxJS operators.
* [rxjs-conduit](https://github.com/Fasteroid/rxjs-conduit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Fasteroid/rxjs-conduit?style=flat)](https://github.com/Fasteroid/rxjs-conduit/stargazers) - RxJS ReplaySubjects with with additional features to make reactive programming easier.
* [rxjs-course](https://github.com/angular-university/rxjs-course) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/angular-university/rxjs-course?style=flat)](https://github.com/angular-university/rxjs-course/stargazers) - RxJS course from Angular University.
* [subscribable-things](https://github.com/chrisguttandin/subscribable-things) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/chrisguttandin/subscribable-things?style=flat)](https://github.com/chrisguttandin/subscribable-things/stargazers) - A collection of reactive wrappers for various browser APIs.
* [subsiphon](https://github.com/shobeiry/subsiphon) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/shobeiry/subsiphon?style=flat)](https://github.com/shobeiry/subsiphon/stargazers) - Lightweight utility for managing multiple RxJS subscriptions with indexed/named keys and simple cleanup methods.
* [web-serial-rxjs](https://github.com/gurezo/web-serial-rxjs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gurezo/web-serial-rxjs?style=flat)](https://github.com/gurezo/web-serial-rxjs/stargazers) - A TypeScript library that provides a reactive RxJS-based wrapper for the Web Serial API, enabling easy serial port communication in web applications.

## Framework Interoperability

### Cross-Framework Integration

* [detector](https://github.com/kitium-ai/detector) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kitium-ai/detector?style=flat)](https://github.com/kitium-ai/detector/stargazers) - A zero-dependency, TypeScript-first library for fast, universal detection of platforms, frameworks, browsers, and capabilities.
* [@oguimbal/ngx-react](https://github.com/oguimbal/ngx-react) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/oguimbal/ngx-react?style=flat)](https://github.com/oguimbal/ngx-react/stargazers) - Enables smooth integration of React and Angular components, or effortless migration between the two.
* [ngx-reactify](https://github.com/knackstedt/ngx-reactify) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/knackstedt/ngx-reactify?style=flat)](https://github.com/knackstedt/ngx-reactify/stargazers) - Library to make running Angular and React applications together easy.
* [ng-react-bridge](https://github.com/john310897/ng-react-bridge) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/john310897/ng-react-bridge?style=flat)](https://github.com/john310897/ng-react-bridge/stargazers) - A lightweight Angular package that enables developers to seamlessly render React components inside Angular components using a directive.
* [gong](https://github.com/fullstack-lang/gong) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fullstack-lang/gong?style=flat)](https://github.com/fullstack-lang/gong/stargazers) - Full‑stack framework with Go (Gin, Gorm, pure SQLite) backend and Angular Material frontend.
* [@retejs/angular-plugin](https://github.com/retejs/angular-plugin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/retejs/angular-plugin?style=flat)](https://github.com/retejs/angular-plugin/stargazers) - Angular plugin with a classic preset of node, connection, socket, and control components, built on [Rete.js](https://retejs.org/).
* [Stencil](https://stenciljs.com/docs/angular) - Generate Angular component wrappers for your web components.
* [AnQst](https://github.com/DusteDdk/AnQst) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DusteDdk/AnQst?style=flat)](https://github.com/DusteDdk/AnQst/stargazers) - Generates Angular services and native Qt widgets from a shared DSL, letting Angular apps compile into QWidget‑based C++ UIs via the AnQst CLI and host libraries.
* [rozie.js](https://github.com/One-Learning-Community/rozie.js) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/One-Learning-Community/rozie.js?style=flat)](https://github.com/One-Learning-Community/rozie.js/stargazers) - A cross-framework compiler that transforms single Vue/Alpine-flavored component files into native Angular code without runtime overhead or wrapper boilerplate.

### External Integration

* [Sentry](https://docs.sentry.io/platforms/javascript/guides/angular/configuration/integrations/) - A developer-first error tracking and performance monitoring platform.

### Wrappers

## Angular-Inspired Solutions

* [angular-style-injector](https://github.com/emmat-york/angular-style-injector) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/emmat-york/angular-style-injector?style=flat)](https://github.com/emmat-york/angular-style-injector/stargazers) - A lightweight dependency injection container inspired by Angular's Injector.
* [di](https://github.com/kaokei/di) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kaokei/di?style=flat)](https://github.com/kaokei/di/stargazers) - This library is a lightweight dependency injection library, similar to [InversifyJS](https://github.com/inversify/InversifyJS) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/inversify/InversifyJS?style=flat)](https://github.com/inversify/InversifyJS/stargazers) and [typedi](https://github.com/typestack/typedi) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/typestack/typedi?style=flat)](https://github.com/typestack/typedi/stargazers).
* [flexdi](https://github.com/AndreyShashlovDev/flexdi) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AndreyShashlovDev/flexdi?style=flat)](https://github.com/AndreyShashlovDev/flexdi/stargazers) - Flexible, lightweight DI library for React, React Native, and Vue3, inspired by NestJS and Angular.
* [gapi](https://github.com/Stradivario/gapi) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Stradivario/gapi?style=flat)](https://github.com/Stradivario/gapi/stargazers) - Inspired by Angular and intended to provide complex Node.js GraphQL Backend applications with minimal effort.
* [GTPL](https://github.com/garag-lib/GTPL) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/garag-lib/GTPL?style=flat)](https://github.com/garag-lib/GTPL/stargazers) - TypeScript library for reactive templates using Direct DOM and Proxy, inspired by Vue, Angular AOT, and JSX, in a compact 9KB package.
* [illuma](https://github.com/git-illuma/core) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/git-illuma/core?style=flat)](https://github.com/git-illuma/core/stargazers) - Angular-style dependency injection for TypeScript.
* [indulgent](https://github.com/frodi-karlsson/indulgent) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/frodi-karlsson/indulgent?style=flat)](https://github.com/frodi-karlsson/indulgent/stargazers) - A lightweight set of TypeScript utilities designed for web development, free of external dependencies and optimized for solid runtime performance.
* [injection-js](https://github.com/mgechev/injection-js) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mgechev/injection-js?style=flat)](https://github.com/mgechev/injection-js/stargazers) - A fast, well‑tested JavaScript/TypeScript dependency injection library extracted from Angular’s `ReflectiveInjector`.
* [ioc](https://github.com/Isqanderm/ioc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Isqanderm/ioc?style=flat)](https://github.com/Isqanderm/ioc/stargazers) - A powerful and flexible Inversion of Control (IoC) container for TypeScript applications. Inspired by Angular and NestJS.
* [knifecycle](https://github.com/nfroidure/knifecycle) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nfroidure/knifecycle?style=flat)](https://github.com/nfroidure/knifecycle/stargazers) - Manage your Node.js processes' lifecycle automatically with an unobtrusive dependency injection implementation.
* [Lua-Generate](https://github.com/Gabriel-c0Nsp/Lua-Generate) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Gabriel-c0Nsp/Lua-Generate?style=flat)](https://github.com/Gabriel-c0Nsp/Lua-Generate/stargazers) - A CLI tool to generate boilerplate code inspired by ng tool from Angular.
* [named-slots](https://github.com/maybebot/named-slots) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/maybebot/named-slots?style=flat)](https://github.com/maybebot/named-slots/stargazers) - Declarative "holes" for React components, inspired by slots in Vue, Svelte, Angular, and WebComponents.
* [needle-di](https://github.com/needle-di/needle-di) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/needle-di/needle-di?style=flat)](https://github.com/needle-di/needle-di/stargazers) - A lightweight, type-safe Dependency Injection (DI) library for JavaScript and TypeScript projects.
* [npm-clang-format-node](https://github.com/lumirlumir/npm-clang-format-node) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lumirlumir/npm-clang-format-node?style=flat)](https://github.com/lumirlumir/npm-clang-format-node/stargazers) - Node wrapper for LLVM Clang's clang-format and git-clang-format native binaries inspired by [clang-format](https://github.com/angular/clang-format) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/angular/clang-format?style=flat)](https://github.com/angular/clang-format/stargazers).
* [ozean](https://github.com/ozeanjs/ozean) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ozeanjs/ozean?style=flat)](https://github.com/ozeanjs/ozean/stargazers) - A modern, simple, and high-performance web framework built on the Bun runtime. It provides a development experience and architecture that should be familiar to Angular users.

* [reaktiv](https://github.com/buiapp/reaktiv) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/buiapp/reaktiv?style=flat)](https://github.com/buiapp/reaktiv/stargazers) - Reactive Signals for Python with first-class async support, inspired by Angular's reactivity model.
* [rgenex](https://github.com/asengar14/rgenex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/asengar14/rgenex?style=flat)](https://github.com/asengar14/rgenex/stargazers) - An Angular‑CLI–style generator for React that instantly scaffolds components, hooks, and pages.
* [rxor](https://github.com/nsevendev/rxor) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nsevendev/rxor?style=flat)](https://github.com/nsevendev/rxor/stargazers) - Brings reactive signals to React, inspired by Angular Signals, Vue 3's `ref/computed`, and SolidJS.
* [Signals](https://github.com/dmytrodemchenko/Signals) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dmytrodemchenko/Signals?style=flat)](https://github.com/dmytrodemchenko/Signals/stargazers) - Zero‑dependency, glitch‑free reactive signals for TypeScript and JavaScript using an optimized Angular‑inspired push/pull architecture.
* [sio](https://github.com/silicia-apps/sio) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/silicia-apps/sio?style=flat)](https://github.com/silicia-apps/sio/stargazers) - Silicia Framework: a fresh approach built upon Ionic, designed to streamline the development of hybrid applications and websites.
* [UnReact.js](https://github.com/arnvjshi/unreactpjs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/arnvjshi/unreactpjs?style=flat)](https://github.com/arnvjshi/unreactpjs/stargazers) - A modern framework combining the best of Angular and React for enhanced component communication.
* [use-vue-service](https://github.com/kaokei/use-vue-service) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kaokei/use-vue-service?style=flat)](https://github.com/kaokei/use-vue-service/stargazers) - Lightweight Vue 3 state management with dependency injection, inspired by Angular services.
